msg:We chose this hotel to be close to the airport. It’s a curious place: interesting ‘hollow square’ shape and filled with various restaurants, shops bars etc. There’s a mall directly opposite that caters to most needs. The room was fine but the decoration is old. Bath and shower very average. The airport proximity is useful but it also means you get a lot of noise from aircraft taking off - they start at 6am and don’t stop until after midnight. So don’t expect a lie in.

In all, it’s good enough for the price, but not up to the quality of 5* hotels elsewhere in Xiamen.
